   <div class="container home">
    <div class="row" style="border-bottom: 1px solid #999999; padding-top:20px; padding-bottom:20px; ">
     <div class="col-sm-5">
      <h4 style="font-size:20px; margin-top:6px; font-weight: bold;">
       Partner with PASCO
      </h4>
      <h4 style="line-height:135%; font-style:italic; color:#777; ">
       <strong>
        Bringing out the scientist in everyone.
       </strong>
      </h4>
      <p style="font-size:16px; margin-top:6px; ">
       Our hands-on probeware and data logging solutions connect your students directly to science and STEM concepts with classroom technology such as sensors, interfaces and data collection and analysis software. We also design and manufacture high quality lab equipment for physics and engineering.
      </p>
     </div>
     <div class="col-sm-7 verticalRuleLeft" style="padding-left:24px; ">
      <div class="col-sm-12">
       <h4 style="font-size:24px; margin-top:0; margin-bottom:12px; ">
        <a href="/digital-library/">
         Digital Library
        </a>
       </h4>
      </div>
      <div class="col-sm-5">
       <a href="/digital-library/">
        <img alt="PASCO Digital Library" class="img-responsive" src="images/Site/Home/Digital-Library-2.png" style="border:1px solid #bbb; "/>
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="col-sm-7">
       <p style="font-size:16px; margin-top:6px; ">
